   <script>
    $(function() {
 	var t=setTimeout(function(){
 		var tweets = "";
 		var cnt = 0;
 		$('#tweetsImport').html( $('#tweets').find('.twitter-timeline-rendered').contents().find('.timeline-Viewport') );
 		
 		$('.timeline-Tweet-text').each(function(index, element)
 		{
 			if (cnt < 5) 
 			{
 				tweets += $.trim($(this).html())+'<span class="seperator"></span>';
 				cnt ++;
 			}
 		});
 
 		$('.twitterTicker').html('');
 		$('.twitterTicker').html(tweets);
 		$('.twitterTicker').marquee({
 			duplicated: true,
 			duration: 30000,
 			gap : 0,
 		});
 		
 		$('.link').attr('target', '_blank');		
 	},1000)
 });
 
 $(function() {
 	
 })
 
 $(function() {
 	resizeWindow();
 })
 	
 $(window).scroll(function() {	
 	resizeWindow();
 });
 	
 $(window).resize(function() {	
 	resizeWindow();
 });
 	
 function resizeWindow() {
 	var scroll = $(window).scrollTop();
 	var height = $('#topBanner').css('height');
 	var headerHeight = $('#header').outerHeight();
 	
 	$('#headerSpacer').css('height', (headerHeight-1)+'px');
 	
 	height = height.replace('px', '');
 	
 	if(scroll <= 0)
 	{
 		$('#fixedHeader').removeClass('scroll');
 		$('#fixedHeader').css('top', (height-1)+'px');
 	}
 	else
 	{
 		$('#fixedHeader').addClass('scroll');
 
 		if((height - scroll) < 0)
 		{
 			$('#fixedHeader').css('top', '0px')
 		}
 		else
 		{
 			$('#fixedHeader').css('top', (height - scroll)+'px')
 		}
 	}
 }
   </script>

    <script>
     var advancedRegionsUrl = '';
 var estate;
 var searchText;
 
 $('#searchSbmt').click(function(e) {
 	e.preventDefault();
 	
 	var url;	
 	var propertyType = $('#propertyType').val();
 	
 	switch(propertyType) {
 		case 'Retail':
 			url = '/shops-to-rent';
 			filter = 'retail';
 			break;
 		case 'Pop-Up Retail':
 			url = '/pop-up-retail';
 			filter = 'pop-up retail';
 			break;
 		case 'Industrial or Warehousing':
 			url = '/industrial-units-to-let';
 			filter = 'industrial or warehousing';
 			break;
 		case 'Offices':
 			url = '/offices-to-rent';
 			filter = 'offices';
 			break;
 		case 'Leisure':
 			url = '/leisure';
 			filter = 'leisure';
 			break;
 		case 'Land':
 			url = '/land';
 			filter = 'land';
 			break;
 		case 'development':
 			url = '/portfolio';
 			filter = 'development';
 			break;
 		case 'Opportunities':
 			url = '/opportunities';
 			filter = 'opportunities';
 			break;
 		case 'Other':
 			url = '/portfolio';
 			filter = 'other';
 			break;
 		case 'Storage':
 			url = '/specialist-storage-facilities';
 			filter = 'storage';
 			break;
 		default:
 			url = '/portfolio';
 			filter = '';
 			break;
 	}
 	
 	var noAdvanced = $('#advancedSearchFieldset').attr('disabled');
 	
 	if(noAdvanced)
 	{
 		url += '/1/'+filter+'/sqft/0-100000/_/_/';
 	}
 	else
 	{
 		var minSize = $('#minSize').val();
 		var maxSize = $('#maxSize').val();
 		
 		url += '/1/'+filter+'/sqft/'+minSize+'-'+maxSize+'/0/'+advancedRegionsUrl+'/';
 	}
 	
 	searchText = $('#searchText').val();
 	
 	/*if(searchText && (estate != 'undefined' && estate != ''))
 	{
 		url += searchText+'|'+estate+'/grid/';
 	}
 	else
 	{*/
 		url += searchText+'/grid/';
 	/*}*/
 	
 	window.location.href = url;
 	//console.log(url);
 });
 
 $('#propertyType').selectmenu({
 	icons: { button: "arrow" }
 });
 
 $('#sizeRange').slider({
 	range: true,
 	min: 0,
 	max: 100000,
 	values: [0, 100000],
 	slide: function( event, ui ) {
 		$('#minSize').val(ui.values[0]);
 		$('#maxSize').val(ui.values[1]);
 	}
 });
 
 $('#minSize').on('keyup', function() {
 	var val = $(this).val();
 	$('#sizeRange').slider('values', 0, val);
 });
 
 $('#maxSize').on('keyup', function() {
 	var val = $(this).val();
 	$('#sizeRange').slider('values', 1, val);
 });
 
 $('#advancedSbmt').click(function(e) {
 	e.preventDefault();
 	
 	if($('#advancedSearchFieldset').is(':disabled'))
 	{
 		$('#advancedSearchFieldset').prop('disabled', false);
 	}
 	else
 	{
 		$('#advancedSearchFieldset').prop('disabled', true);
 	}
 	
 	$('#advancedSearch').stop().slideToggle(600, 'easeOutCubic')
 });
 
 
 $('#searchText').autocomplete({
 	source: function(request, response) {
 		var propertyType = $('#propertyType').val();
     	$.getJSON('/widgets/search-autocomplete.php', {
 			term: $('#searchText').val(),
 			type: $('#propertyType').val()
 		}, response);
 	},
 	minLength: 2,
 });
 
 $('#searchText').on('autocompletefocus', function(e, ui) {
 	e.preventDefault();
 	$('#searchText').val(ui.item.val);
 });
 
 $('#searchText').on('autocompleteselect', function(e, ui) {
 	e.preventDefault();
 	$('#searchText').val(ui.item.val);
 	console.log(ui)
 });
 
 $('.regionCheckbox').click(function(e) {
 	e.preventDefault();
 	
 	var id = $(this).attr('id');
 	var field = $(this).attr('id').replace('Check', '');
 	
 	console.log(id);
 	
 	if($('#'+id).hasClass('checked'))
 	{
 		$('#'+id).removeClass('checked');
 		$('#'+field).val(0);
 	}
 	else
 	{
 		$('#'+id).addClass('checked');
 		$('#'+field).val(1);
 	}
 	
 	advancedRegionsUrl = '';
 	
 	$('.advancedRegion').each(function(index, element) {
 		var obj = $.makeArray(element);
 		var reg = obj[0]['attributes'].arid.nodeValue;
 		var val = obj[0].value;
 		
 		if(val == 1)
 		{
 			advancedRegionsUrl += reg+'_';
 		}
     });
 	
 	console.log(advancedRegionsUrl);
 	
 });
 
 $('.regionsList').click(function(e) {
 	e.preventDefault();
 	var id = '#'+$(this).attr('for');
 	$(id).click();
 });
 	
 var searchPosition;
 	
 $(function() {
 	searchPosition = $('#search').position();
 });
 	
 $(window).scroll(function() {
 	var scroll = $(this).scrollTop();	
 	var top = $('#fixedHeader').css('height');
 	top = top.replace('px', '');
 	
 	if(searchPosition.top <= (parseInt(scroll)+parseInt(top)))
 	{
 		$('#search').addClass('fixed');
 		$('#search').css('top', parseInt(top)+'px');
 		
 		var searchHeight = $('#search').outerHeight();
 		
 		$('#searchSpacer').css('height', searchHeight+'px');
 	}
 	else
 	{
 		$('#search').removeClass('fixed');
 		$('#search').css('top', 0);
 		$('#searchSpacer').css('height', 0);
 	}
 });
    </script>
   </div>

        </div>
        <script>
         $('.lazy.image').lazyload({
 		effect:"fadeIn",
 	});
 	
 	$('.more.btn').click(function() {
 		var id = $(this).attr('show');
 		$(this).fadeOut('fast', function() {
 			$('#'+id).fadeIn('fast')
 		});
 	});
 	
 	$('.enquire').click(function(e) {
 		var property = $(this).closest('.property');
 		var unit = $(this).attr('unit');
 		$('.enquiryForm').slideUp('fast');
 		
 		if($('.enquiryForm').attr('unit') == unit)
 		{
 			property.find('.enquiryForm').attr('unit', '');
 		}
 		else
 		{
 			property.find('.enquiryForm').attr('unit', unit);
 			
 			$.ajax({
 				method:'POST',
 				cache:false,
 				url:'/widgets/ajax.enquiry-form.php',
 				data: {
 					unit:unit,
 				}
 			}).done(function(data) {
 				property.find('.enquiryForm').html(data);
 				property.find('.enquiryForm').slideDown('fast');
 			});
 		}
 		
 		e.stopPropagation();
 	});
        </script>
